DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  # Set up environment
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      git \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      rpm-build \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      od \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Python tools
  RUN pip3 install pipenv virtualenv
  # Install jq from source
  RUN wget https://github.com/stedolan/jq/releases/latest/download/jq-linux64 -O /usr/local/bin/jq \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/jq
  # Clone and build decNumber library
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  # Copy repository files
  COPY . /root/
  # Build from source if needed (uncomment if required)
  # RUN ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
  #     && make \
  #     && make install
  # Set up bash environment
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  # Set up environment
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  # Install system dependencies with retries and error handling
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      rpm-build \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      od \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Python tools
  RUN pip3 install --no-cache-dir pipenv virtualenv
  # Install jq from source
  RUN wget --no-verbose https://github.com/stedolan/jq/releases/latest/download/jq-linux64 -O /usr/local/bin/jq \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/jq
  # Clone and build decNumber library
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  # Copy repository files
  COPY . /root/
  # Configure and build jq
  RUN ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  # Set up bash environment
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 2 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip3 install --no-cache-dir pipenv virtualenv
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip3 install --no-cache-dir pipenv virtualenv
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      apt-transport-https \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm main contrib non-free" > /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm-updates main contrib non-free" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://security.debian.org/debian-security bookworm-security main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-pipenv \
      python3-virtualenv \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      apt-transport-https \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm main contrib non-free" > /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm-updates main contrib non-free" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://security.debian.org/debian-security bookworm-security main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-pipenv \
      python3-virtualenv \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      apt-transport-https \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm main contrib non-free" > /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm-updates main contrib non-free" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://security.debian.org/debian-security bookworm-security main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN git clone https://github.com/decNumber/decNumber.git \
      && cd decNumber \
      && gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c \
      && ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o \
      && cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ \
      && cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ \
      && ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      apt-transport-https \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm main contrib non-free" > /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm-updates main contrib non-free" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://security.debian.org/debian-security bookworm-security main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY vendor/decNumber /root/vendor/decNumber
  RUN cd vendor/decNumber && \
      gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c && \
      ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o && \
      mkdir -p /usr/local/lib /usr/local/include && \
      cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ && \
      cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ && \
      ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:12-slim
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /root
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      apt-transport-https \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm main contrib non-free" > /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm-updates main contrib non-free" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://security.debian.org/debian-security bookworm-security main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      pkg-config \
      liblz4-dev \
      valgrind \
      rpm \
      gcovr \
      libasan6 \
      libubsan1 \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY vendor/decNumber /root/vendor/decNumber
  RUN cd vendor/decNumber && \
      gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c && \
      ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o && \
      mkdir -p /usr/local/lib /usr/local/include && \
      cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ && \
      cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ && \
      ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libonig-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu --with-oniguruma=builtin \
      && make -j$(nproc) \
      && make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive

  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      ca-certificates \
      apt-transport-https \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm main contrib non-free" > /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bookworm-updates main contrib non-free" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      echo "deb http://security.debian.org/debian-security bookworm-security main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list

      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      libtool \
      make \
      automake \
      autoconf \
      flex \
      bison \

      libubsan1 \
      wget \

      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  COPY vendor/decNumber /root/vendor/decNumber
  RUN cd vendor/decNumber && \
      gcc -m64 -O3 -c decNumber.c decContext.c && \
      ar rcs libdecnumber.a decNumber.o decContext.o && \
      mkdir -p /usr/local/lib /usr/local/include && \
      cp libdecnumber.a /usr/local/lib/ && \
      cp decNumber.h decContext.h /usr/local/include/ && \
      ldconfig
  COPY . /root/
  RUN autoreconf -fi && \
      ./configure --host=x86_64-linux-gnu && \
      make -j$(nproc) && \
      make install
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
